local v_u_1 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v_u_2 = TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
local v_u_3 = TweenInfo.new(0.1, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
local v4 = script.Parent
function getTweens(p5) -- name: getTweens
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_3
	local v6 = p5:GetAttribute("HoverPadding") or 2
	local v7 = p5.Size
	return v_u_1:Create(p5, v_u_2, {
		["Size"] = UDim2.new(v7.X.Scale, v7.X.Offset + v6, v7.Y.Scale, v7.Y.Offset + v6)
	}), v_u_1:Create(p5, v_u_3, {
		["Size"] = v7
	})
end
function handleDescendant(p8) -- name: handleDescendant
	if p8.Name ~= "Profile" or p8.Parent.Name ~= "Right" then
		if p8:IsA("TextButton") or p8:IsA("ImageButton") then
			if p8:GetAttribute("DONT_ANIMATE") then
				return
			end
			local v9
			if p8:FindFirstChild("Container") then
				v9 = p8.Container
			else
				v9 = p8
			end
			local v_u_10, v_u_11 = getTweens(v9)
			local v_u_12 = false
			p8.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_10
				if not v_u_12 then
					v_u_12 = true
					v_u_10:Play()
				end
			end)
			p8.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
				v_u_12 = false
				v_u_11:Play()
			end)
			p8.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
				v_u_12 = false
				v_u_11:Play()
			end)
		end
	end
end
for _, v13 in pairs(v4:GetDescendants()) do
	handleDescendant(v13)
end
v4.DescendantAdded:Connect(handleDescendant)

local v_u_2 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v_u_3 = game:GetService("StarterGui")

local v_u_5 = require(v4:WaitForChild("Info"))
local v_u_6 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
function v_u_1.CaseInfo(p7) -- name: CaseInfo
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_5
	local v8, v9 = v_u_1.CustomCase(p7)
	local v10 = {}
	for v11, v12 in v8 do
		table.insert(v10, { v11, v12 })
	end
	table.sort(p7, function(p13, p14)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_5
		return v_u_5.Gifts[p13].Price > v_u_5.Gifts[p14].Price
	end)
	return {
		["Price"] = nil,
		["Image"] = "126118629758124",
		["Drop"] = nil,
		["Custom"] = true,
		["Top3"] = nil,
		["Price"] = v9,
		["Drop"] = v10,
		["Top3"] = { p7[1], p7[2], p7[3] }
	}
end
function v_u_1.CustomCase(p15) -- name: CustomCase
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_1
	local v16 = (1 / 0)
	local v17 = {}
	local v18 = 0
	local v19 = {}
	local v20 = ""
	for _, v21 in p15 do
		local v22 = v_u_5.Gifts[v21]
		if v22.Price < v16 then
			v16 = v22.Price
			v20 = v21
		end
	end
	for _, v23 in p15 do
		local v24 = 1 / (v_u_5.Gifts[v23].Price / v16)
		v17[v23] = v24
		v18 = v18 + v24
	end
	for _, v25 in p15 do
		local v26 = v17[v25] / v18 * 100000
		local v27 = math.round(v26) / 1000
		local _ = v17[v25] / v18 * 100
		v19[v25] = v27
	end
	local v28 = 0
	for _, v29 in p15 do
		local v30 = (v28 + v19[v29]) * 1000
		v28 = math.round(v30) / 1000
	end
	local v31 = 100 - v28
	v19[v20] = v19[v20] + v31
	local v32 = 0
	local v33 = 0
	for _, v34 in p15 do
		v32 = v32 + v19[v34] / 100 * v_u_5.Gifts[v34].Price
		local v35 = (v33 + v19[v34]) * 1000
		v33 = math.round(v35) / 1000
	end
	local v36 = v_u_1.GetROI1(v32)
	local v37 = math.round(v32) / v36 / 5
	return v19, math.round(v37) * 5
end
function v_u_1.GetROI1(p38) -- name: GetROI1
	local v39 = math.min(500000000, p38)
	return (math.max(2000000, v39) - 2000000) / 498000000 * -0.25 + 0.85
end
function v_u_1.GetROI(p40) -- name: GetROI
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5
	local v_u_41 = v_u_5.Cases[p40].Drop
	local v_u_42 = v_u_5.Cases[p40].Price
	table.sort(v_u_41, function(p43, p44)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_5
		return v_u_5.Gifts[p43[1]].Price < v_u_5.Gifts[p44[1]].Price
	end)
	local function v50(p45) -- name: E
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_41, (ref) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_42
		local v46 = 0
		local v47 = 0
		for v48 = 1, #v_u_41 do
			local v49 = v_u_41[v48][2] / 100
			v47 = v47 + ((v46 + v49) ^ p45 - v46 ^ p45) * v_u_5.Gifts[v_u_41[v48][1]].Price
			v46 = v46 + v49
		end
		return v47 / v_u_42
	end
	return v50(1), v50(2), v50(4)
end
function v_u_1.GroupTransparency(p51, p52, p53) -- name: GroupTransparency
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2
	local v54 = p51:GetDescendants()
	table.insert(v54, p51)
	for _, v55 in v54 do
		if v55:IsA("TextLabel") then
			if p53 then
				v_u_2:Create(v55, TweenInfo.new(p53), {
					["TextTransparency"] = p52
				}):Play()
			else
				v55.TextTransparency = p52
			end
		elseif v55:IsA("ImageLabel") then
			if p53 then
				v_u_2:Create(v55, TweenInfo.new(p53), {
					["ImageTransparency"] = p52
				}):Play()
			else
				v55.ImageTransparency = p52
			end
		end
		if v55:IsA("GuiObject") then
			if p53 then
				v_u_2:Create(v55, TweenInfo.new(p53), {
					["BackgroundTransparency"] = p52
				}):Play()
			else
				v55.BackgroundTransparency = p52
			end
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.SimpleNumber(p56) -- name: SimpleNumber
	local v57 = math.floor(p56)
	local v58 = tostring(v57)
	repeat
		local v59
		v58, v59 = string.gsub(v58, "^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", "%1,%2")
	until v59 == 0
	return v58
end
function v_u_1.CreateSound(p60, p61) -- name: CreateSound
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	if not (p61 and (p61:IsA("Frame") or p61:IsA("ScrollingFrame"))) or p61.Visible then
		local v62 = p60:Clone()
		v62.Parent = p61 or v_u_6.PlayerGui
		v62:Play()
		game.Debris:AddItem(v62, v62.TimeLength)
		return v62
	end
end
function v_u_1.CreatePitchSound(p63, p64, p65) -- name: CreatePitchSound
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	if not (p65 and (p65:IsA("Frame") or p65:IsA("ScrollingFrame"))) or p65.Visible then
		local v66 = p63:Clone()
		v66.Parent = p65 or v_u_6.PlayerGui
		local v67 = Instance.new("PitchShiftSoundEffect")
		v67.Parent = v66
		v67.Octave = p64
		v66:Play()
		game.Debris:AddItem(v66, v66.TimeLength)
		return v66
	end
end
function v_u_1.Notify(p68, p69, p70) -- name: Notify
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_3
	if p70 then
		v_u_1.CreateSound(p70)
	end
	v_u_3:SetCore("SendNotification", {
		["Title"] = p68,
		["Text"] = p69
	})
end
function v_u_1.SortedGifts() -- name: SortedGifts
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5
	local v71 = {}
	for v72, v73 in v_u_5.Gifts do
		local v74 = table.clone(v73)
		v74.Name = v72
		table.insert(v71, v74)
	end
	table.sort(v71, function(p75, p76)
		return p75.Price < p76.Price
	end)
	local v77 = {}
	for _, v78 in v71 do
		local v79 = v78.Name
		table.insert(v77, v79)
	end
	return v77
end
return v_u_1

local v_u_1 = {
	["Sliders"] = {}
}
local v2 = game:GetService("RunService")
local v_u_3 = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local v_u_4 = game:GetService("TweenService")
local v5 = v2:IsClient()
assert(v5, "Slider module can only be used on the Client!")
local v6 = script.Utils
local v_u_7 = require(v6.Signal)
local v_u_8 = require(v6.SliderFuncs)
function v_u_1.__index(p9, p10)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	local v11 = {
		{ ".OnChange", ".Changed", (rawget(p9, "Changed")) }
	}
	for _, v12 in ipairs(v11) do
		local v13 = v12[1]
		if string.sub(v13, 2) == p10 then
			warn(string.format("%s is deprecated, please use %s instead", v12[1], v12[2]))
			return v12[3]
		end
	end
	return v_u_1[p10]
end
function v_u_1.new(p_u_14, p15) -- name: new
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_7
	local v16 = pcall(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_14
		return p_u_14.AbsoluteSize, p_u_14.AbsolutePosition
	end)
	assert(v16, "Holder argument does not have an AbsoluteSize/AbsolutePosition")
	local v17 = false
	for _, v18 in ipairs(v_u_1.Sliders) do
		if v18._holder == p_u_14 then
			v17 = true
			break
		end
	end
	assert(not v17, "Cannot set two sliders with same frame!")
	local v19 = p15.SliderData.Increment ~= nil
	assert(v19, "Failed to find Increment in SliderData table")
	local v20 = p15.SliderData.Start ~= nil
	assert(v20, "Failed to find Start in SliderData table")
	local v21 = p15.SliderData.End ~= nil
	assert(v21, "Failed to find End in SliderData table")
	local v22 = p15.SliderData.Increment > 0
	assert(v22, "SliderData.Increment must be greater than 0")
	local v23 = p15.SliderData.End > p15.SliderData.Start
	local v24 = string.format
	local v25 = p15.SliderData.End
	local v26 = p15.SliderData.Start
	assert(v23, v24("Slider end value must be greater than its start value! (%.1f <= %.1f)", v25, v26))
	local v27 = v_u_1
	local v_u_28 = setmetatable({}, v27)
	v_u_28._holder = p_u_14
	v_u_28._data = {
		["Button"] = nil,
		["HolderButton"] = nil,
		["_clickOverride"] = false,
		["_mainConnection"] = nil,
		["_clickConnections"] = nil,
		["_otherConnections"] = nil,
		["_inputPos"] = nil,
		["_percent"] = 0,
		["_value"] = 0,
		["_scaleIncrement"] = 0,
		["_currentTween"] = nil,
		["_allowBackgroundClick"] = nil,
		["_clickConnections"] = {},
		["_otherConnections"] = {},
		["_allowBackgroundClick"] = p15.AllowBackgroundClick ~= false
	}
	v_u_28._config = p15
	v_u_28._config.Axis = string.upper(p15.Axis or "X")
	v_u_28._config.Padding = p15.Padding or 2
	v_u_28._config.MoveInfo = p15.MoveInfo or TweenInfo.new(0.2)
	v_u_28._config.MoveType = p15.MoveType or "Tween"
	v_u_28.IsHeld = false
	local v29 = p_u_14:FindFirstChild("Circle")
	local v30 = v29 ~= nil
	assert(v30, "Failed to find slider button.")
	local v31 = v29:IsA("GuiButton")
	assert(v31, "Slider is not a GuiButton")
	v_u_28._data.Button = v29
	if v_u_28._data._allowBackgroundClick then
		local v32 = Instance.new("TextButton")
		v32.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		v32.Text = ""
		v32.Name = "HolderClickButton"
		v32.Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 1)
		v32.ZIndex = -1
		v32.Parent = v_u_28._holder
		v_u_28._data.HolderButton = v32
	end
	v_u_28._data._percent = 0
	if p15.SliderData.DefaultValue then
		local v33 = p15.SliderData
		local v34 = p15.SliderData.DefaultValue
		local v35 = p15.SliderData.Start
		local v36 = p15.SliderData.End
		v33.DefaultValue = math.clamp(v34, v35, v36)
		v_u_28._data._percent = v_u_8.getAlphaBetween(p15.SliderData.Start, p15.SliderData.End, p15.SliderData.DefaultValue)
	end
	local v37 = v_u_28._data
	local v38 = v_u_28._data._percent
	v37._percent = math.clamp(v38, 0, 1)
	v_u_28._data._value = v_u_8.getNewValue(v_u_28)
	v_u_28._data._increment = p15.SliderData.Increment
	v_u_28._data._scaleIncrement = v_u_8.getScaleIncrement(v_u_28)
	v_u_28.Changed = v_u_7.new()
	v_u_28.Dragged = v_u_7.new()
	v_u_28.Released = v_u_7.new()
	v_u_28._data._percent = v_u_8.snapToScale(v_u_28._data._percent, v_u_28._data._scaleIncrement)
	v_u_28:Move()
	local v39 = v_u_28._data._otherConnections
	local v40 = v29:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteSize")
	table.insert(v39, v40:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_28
		v_u_28:Move("Instant")
	end))
	local v41 = v_u_1.Sliders
	table.insert(v41, v_u_28)
	return v_u_28
end
function v_u_1.Track(p_u_42) -- name: Track
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3
	for _, v43 in ipairs(p_u_42._data._clickConnections) do
		v43:Disconnect()
	end
	local v44 = p_u_42._data._clickConnections
	local v45 = p_u_42._data.Button.MouseButton1Down
	table.insert(v44, v45:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_42
		p_u_42.IsHeld = true
	end))
	local v46 = p_u_42._data._clickConnections
	local v47 = p_u_42._data.Button.MouseButton1Up
	table.insert(v46, v47:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_42
		if p_u_42.IsHeld then
			p_u_42.Released:Fire(p_u_42._data._value)
		end
		p_u_42.IsHeld = false
	end))
	if p_u_42._data._allowBackgroundClick then
		local v48 = p_u_42._data._clickConnections
		local v49 = p_u_42._data.HolderButton.Activated
		table.insert(v48, v49:Connect(function(p50)
			-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_42
			if p50.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or p50.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
				p_u_42._data._inputPos = p50.Position
				p_u_42._data._clickOverride = true
				p_u_42:Update()
				p_u_42._data._clickOverride = false
			end
		end))
	end
	if p_u_42.Changed then
		p_u_42.Changed:Fire(p_u_42._data._value)
	end
	if p_u_42._data._mainConnection then
		p_u_42._data._mainConnection:Disconnect()
	end
	p_u_42._data._mainConnection = v_u_3.InputChanged:Connect(function(p51, _)
		-- upvalues: (copy) p_u_42
		if p51.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or p51.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
			p_u_42._data._inputPos = p51.Position
			p_u_42:Update()
		end
	end)
end
function v_u_1.Update(p52) -- name: Update
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
	if (p52.IsHeld or p52._data._clickOverride) and p52._data._inputPos then
		local v53 = p52._holder.AbsoluteSize[p52._config.Axis]
		local v54 = p52._holder.AbsolutePosition[p52._config.Axis]
		local v55 = p52._data._inputPos[p52._config.Axis]
		if v55 then
			local v56 = v55 - v54
			local v57 = v_u_8.snapToScale(v56 / v53, p52._data._scaleIncrement)
			local v58 = math.clamp(v57, 0, 1)
			p52._data._percent = v58
			p52.Dragged:Fire(p52._data._value)
			p52:Move()
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.Untrack(p59) -- name: Untrack
	for _, v60 in ipairs(p59._data._clickConnections) do
		v60:Disconnect()
	end
	if p59._data._mainConnection then
		p59._data._mainConnection:Disconnect()
	end
	p59.IsHeld = false
end
function v_u_1.Reset(p61) -- name: Reset
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
	for _, v62 in ipairs(p61._data._clickConnections) do
		v62:Disconnect()
	end
	if p61._data._mainConnection then
		p61._data._mainConnection:Disconnect()
	end
	p61.IsHeld = false
	p61._data._percent = 0
	if p61._config.SliderData.DefaultValue then
		p61._data._percent = v_u_8.getAlphaBetween(p61._config.SliderData.Start, p61._config.SliderData.End, p61._config.SliderData.DefaultValue)
	end
	local v63 = p61._data
	local v64 = p61._data._percent
	v63._percent = math.clamp(v64, 0, 1)
	p61:Move()
end
function v_u_1.OverrideValue(p65, p66) -- name: OverrideValue
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
	p65.IsHeld = false
	p65._data._percent = v_u_8.getAlphaBetween(p65._config.SliderData.Start, p65._config.SliderData.End, p66)
	local v67 = p65._data
	local v68 = p65._data._percent
	v67._percent = math.clamp(v68, 0, 1)
	p65._data._percent = v_u_8.snapToScale(p65._data._percent, p65._data._scaleIncrement)
	p65:Move()
end
function v_u_1.Move(p69, p70) -- name: Move
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_4
	p69._data._value = v_u_8.getNewValue(p69)
	if p70 == nil then
		p70 = p69._config.MoveType
	end
	if p70 == "Tween" or p70 == nil then
		if p69._data._currentTween then
			p69._data._currentTween:Cancel()
		end
		p69._data._currentTween = v_u_4:Create(p69._data.Button, p69._config.MoveInfo, {
			["Position"] = v_u_8.getNewPosition(p69)
		})
		p69._data._currentTween:Play()
	elseif p70 == "Instant" then
		p69._data.Button.Position = v_u_8.getNewPosition(p69)
	end
	p69.Changed:Fire(p69._data._value)
end
function v_u_1.OverrideIncrement(p71, p72) -- name: OverrideIncrement
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_8
	p71._config.SliderData.Increment = p72
	p71._data._increment = p72
	p71._data._scaleIncrement = v_u_8.getScaleIncrement(p71)
	local v73 = p71._data
	local v74 = p71._data._percent
	v73._percent = math.clamp(v74, 0, 1)
	p71._data._percent = v_u_8.snapToScale(p71._data._percent, p71._data._scaleIncrement)
	p71:Move()
end
function v_u_1.GetValue(p75) -- name: GetValue
	return p75._data._value
end
function v_u_1.GetIncrement(p76) -- name: GetIncrement
	return p76._data._increment
end
function v_u_1.Destroy(p77) -- name: Destroy
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	for _, v78 in ipairs(p77._data._clickConnections) do
		v78:Disconnect()
	end
	for _, v79 in ipairs(p77._data._otherConnections) do
		v79:Disconnect()
	end
	if p77._data._mainConnection then
		p77._data._mainConnection:Disconnect()
	end
	if p77._data.HolderButton then
		p77._data.HolderButton:Destroy()
		p77._data.HolderButton = nil
	end
	p77.Changed:Destroy()
	p77.Dragged:Destroy()
	p77.Released:Destroy()
	for v80 = 1, #v_u_1.Sliders do
		if v_u_1.Sliders[v80] == p77 then
			table.remove(v_u_1.Sliders, v80)
		end
	end
	setmetatable(p77, nil)
end
v_u_3.InputEnded:Connect(function(p81, _)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	if p81.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or p81.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then

local function v_u_36() -- name: updateXP
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_14

	local v25 = v_u_13.Value

	local v29

		v29 = v28 * 100 + 200
	else
		v29 = v28 * 160 + 500
	end
	v26.Value = v27 / v29 * 100
	local v30 = v_u_11.Frame.Level.xp
	local v31 = v_u_14.Value
	local v32 = tostring(v31)

		v35 = v34 * 100 + 200
	else
		v35 = v34 * 160 + 500
	end
	v30.Text = v32 .. v33 .. tostring(v35) .. "</font>"
end
local function v_u_44(p37, p38, p39) -- name: updateStatus

		v42.Name = v41
		v42.Value = false
		v42.Parent = v_u_16

	local v43 = v_u_15.Value == 1
	if p39 then
		if v43 then
			if p38 < v_u_13.Value then
				v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
				return
			elseif p38 == v_u_13.Value then
				v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
			else
				v40.Image = "rbxassetid://105706361949544"
			end
		else
			v40.Image = "rbxassetid://105706361949544"
			return
		end
	elseif p38 < v_u_13.Value then
		v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
		return
	elseif p38 == v_u_13.Value then
		v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
	else
		v40.Image = "rbxassetid://105706361949544"
	end
end
local function v_u_54(p45, p46) -- name: updateXPBar
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_17
	if p46 <= v_u_13.Value then
		p45.XPBar.Visible = true
		p45.XPBar.Progress.Fill.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		p45.XPBar.Level.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(55, 100, 221)
		p45.LockedXPBar.Visible = false
		return
	elseif p46 == v_u_13.Value + 1 then
		p45.XPBar.Visible = false
		p45.LockedXPBar.Visible = true
		local v47 = v_u_13.Value + 1
		local v48
		if v47 <= 25 then
			v48 = v47 * 100 + 200
		else
			v48 = v47 * 160 + 500
		end
		local v49 = v_u_14.Value / v48
		p45.LockedXPBar.Progress.Fill.Size = UDim2.new(v49, 0, 1, 0)
		p45.LockedXPBar.Level.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(19, 19, 19)
		p45.LockedXPBar.Progress.TextLabel.Text = string.format("<b>%d</b> / <font weight=\'medium\'>%d</font>", v_u_14.Value, v48)
		local v50 = p45.LockedXPBar.Buylvl.TextLabel
		local v51 = "\238\128\130"
		local v52 = p46 - 1
		local v53
		if v52 >= 1 and v52 <= 8 then
			v53 = v_u_17["1-10"]
		elseif v52 >= 9 and v52 <= 18 then
			v53 = v_u_17["11-20"]
		elseif v52 >= 19 and v52 <= 28 then
			v53 = v_u_17["21-30"]
		elseif v52 >= 29 and v52 <= 38 then
			v53 = v_u_17["31-40"]
		elseif v52 >= 39 and v52 < 50 then
			v53 = v_u_17["41-50"]
		else
			v53 = nil
		end
		v50.Text = v51 .. tostring(v53)
	else
		p45.XPBar.Visible = true
		p45.XPBar.Progress.Fill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
		p45.XPBar.Level.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(19, 19, 19)
		p45.LockedXPBar.Visible = false
	end
end

local function v_u_107(p101) -- name: formatReward
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_8
	local v102
	if p101[1] == "snow" then
		v102 = "Snowflakes"
	elseif p101[1] == "gems" then
		v102 = "Gems"
	elseif p101[1] == "ton" then
		v102 = "TON"
	elseif p101[1] == "stars" then
		v102 = "Stars"
	elseif p101[1] == "x2" then
		v102 = "x2 Luck Potion"
	elseif p101[1] == "x4" then
		v102 = "x4 Luck Potion"
	else
		local v103 = p101[2]
		v102 = tostring(v103)
	end
	if p101[1] == "x2" or p101[1] == "x4" then
		local v104 = p101[2] or 1
		return v102 .. " (" .. tostring(v104) .. "sec)", "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_5.Icons[p101[1]]
	end
	if p101[1] == "item" then
		return v102, "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[p101[2]].Image
	end
	if p101[2] then
		local v105 = v_u_8.SimpleNumber
		local v106 = p101[2]
		v102 = v102 .. " (x" .. tostring(v105(v106)) .. ")"
	end
	return v102, "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_5.Icons[p101[1]]
end

local function v_u_141() -- name: update
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_131, (copy) v_u_11
	local v132 = v_u_131 - os.time()
	if v132 <= 432000 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 48, 51)
	elseif v132 <= 0 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = "Ended!"
		return
	end
	local v133 = v132 / 86400
	local v134 = math.floor(v133)
	local v135 = v132 % 86400 / 3600
	local v136 = math.floor(v135)
	local v137 = v132 % 3600 / 60
	local v138 = math.floor(v137)
	local v139 = v132 % 60
	local v140 = math.floor(v139)
	v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = string.format("Ends in: %02d:%02d:%02d:%02d", v134, v136, v138, v140)
	if v132 <= 0 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = "Ended!"
	end
end

v_u_9.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_14
	local v15 = 0
	for _, v16 in v_u_10 do
		v15 = v15 + v16
	end
	if v15 > 10 or v15 < 1 then
		return
	else
		local v17 = {}
		for v18, v19 in v_u_10 do
			for _ = 1, v19 do
				table.insert(v17, v18)
			end
		end
		if #v17 > 10 or #v17 < 1 then
			return
		else
			local v20, v21 = v_u_4.Battles:InvokeServer("Create", v17, {})
			if v20 then
				v_u_7.MainFrame.Visible = false
				v_u_6.Visible = false
				v_u_7:WaitForChild("Battle").Visible = true
				v_u_10 = {}
				for _, v22 in v_u_8:GetChildren() do
					if v22:IsA("Frame") and v22:FindFirstChild("Buttons") then
						v22.Buttons.Selected.Visible = false
					end
				end

				v_u_4.Btl:Fire(v17)
			else
				v_u_3.Notify("ERROR", v21, v_u_5.UI_Error)
			end
		end
	end
end)

local function v_u_25() -- name: GetResultTable
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_6
	local v24 = {
		["FullName"] = v_u_21[2],
		["NFT"] = string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[1]
	}
	if string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[2] then
		v24.Model = string.split(string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[2], ")")[1]
	else
		v24.Model = "Default"
	end
	v24.Owner = v_u_21[3]
	v24.Backdrop = v_u_21[4]
	v24.Color = v_u_6.Backdrops[v_u_21[4]]
	v24.Pattern = v_u_21[5]
	v24.Date = v_u_21[6]
	v24.Number = v_u_21[7]
	return v24
end
local function v_u_33(p26) -- name: radialprogress
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_5
	local v27 = p26 / 100 * 360
	local v28 = v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.Left.Circle
	local v29 = v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.Right.Circle
	if p26 > 0 and p26 <= 50 then
		v29.Visible = false
		v28.Visible = true
		v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180 + v27
		}):Play()
		return
	elseif p26 <= 0 then
		if v29.UIGradient.Rotation ~= -180 then
			local v30 = v_u_5:Create(v29.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
				["Rotation"] = -180
			})
			v30:Play()
			v30.Completed:Wait()
		end
		local v31 = v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180
		})
		v31:Play()
		v31.Completed:Wait()
		v29.Visible = false
		v28.Visible = false
	else
		v28.Visible = true
		v29.Visible = true
		local v32 = v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = 0
		})
		v32:Play()
		v32.Completed:Wait()
		v_u_5:Create(v29.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180 + (v27 - 180)
		}):Play()
	end
end
local function v_u_43() -- name: UpdateSelected
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_14, (ref) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_33
	local v34 = 0
	local v35 = ""
	for v36 = 1, 4 do
		local v37 = v_u_10:FindFirstChild("Frame" .. v36)
		if v_u_16[v36] then
			v37.NFTFrame.NFT.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v_u_16[v36].Name].Image
			for _, v38 in v37.NFTFrame.Patterns:GetChildren() do
				v38.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_14[v_u_16[v36]:GetAttribute("Pattern")]
			end
			v37.NFTFrame.BackgroundColor3 = v_u_6.Backdrops[v_u_16[v36]:GetAttribute("Backdrop")]
			local v39 = (v_u_6.Gifts[v_u_16[v36].Name].Price or 0) / 320000000
			local v40 = math.clamp(v39, 0, 1) * 20 + 5
			local v41 = math.round(v40)
			v34 = v34 + v41
			v37.NFTFrame.Percent.Text = tostring(v41) .. "%"
			v37.NFTFrame.Visible = true
			v35 = string.split(v_u_16[v36].Name, " (")[1]
		else
			v37.NFTFrame.Visible = false
		end
	end
	if #v_u_16 <= 0 then
		v_u_22 = nil
		v35 = ""
	end
	local v42 = math.clamp(v34, 0, 100)
	task.spawn(v_u_33, v42)
	v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.percent.Text = tostring(v42) .. "%"
	v_u_10.Button.Succ.Text = "Success Chance: " .. tostring(v42) .. "%"
	if v_u_22 then
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft " .. v35 .. " " .. v_u_22
	else
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft"
	end
end
local function v_u_46(p44) -- name: SelectGift
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_43
	if not table.find(v_u_16, p44) then
		if v_u_16[1] then
			if string.split(v_u_16[1].Name, " (")[1] == string.split(p44.Name, " (")[1] then
				if #v_u_16 < 4 then
					local v45 = v_u_16
					table.insert(v45, p44)
				end
			else
				v_u_16 = { p44 }
				v_u_22 = string.split(p44:GetAttribute("Number"), " ")[2]
			end
		else
			v_u_16 = { p44 }
			v_u_22 = string.split(p44:GetAttribute("Number"), " ")[2]
		end
		v_u_43()
	end
end

end

			v_u_92.Summer.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_90.Name].Summer

	end

function TableFormat(p54, p55) -- name: TableFormat
	local v56 = {}
	for v57, v58 in ipairs(p54) do
		if v57 ~= p55 then
			table.insert(v56, v58)
		end
	end
	return v56
end

local function v72(p_u_69) -- name: ItemFrame

	if p_u_69:GetAttribute("Unique") then
		return

		if v_u_6.Gifts[v70].Price >= 10000 then
			local v_u_71 = script.InventoryFrame:Clone()
			v_u_71.Name = p_u_69.Name
			v_u_71.Txt.Text = v70

			v_u_71.Summer.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_69.Name].Summer
			p_u_69.Destroying:Connect(function()

			end)
			v_u_71.Button.Activated:Connect(function()

				if not v_u_63 then

				end
			end)
		end
	end

		v32, v33 = string.gsub(v32, "^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", "%1,%2")
	until v33 == 0
	return v32
end

local function v_u_46(p39) -- name: ParseDateString
	local v40, v41, v42, v43, v44, v45 = p39:match("(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+):(%d+):(%d+)")
	return v40 and {
		["year"] = tonumber(v40),
		["month"] = tonumber(v41),
		["day"] = tonumber(v42),
		["hour"] = tonumber(v43),
		["min"] = tonumber(v44),
		["sec"] = tonumber(v45)
	} or nil
end
local function v_u_53(p47) -- name: GetTimeAgo
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_46
	if type(p47) == "string" then
		p47 = v_u_46(p47)
	end
	if type(p47) ~= "table" then
		return "Unknown time"
	end
	local v48 = os.time({
		["year"] = p47.year,
		["month"] = p47.month,
		["day"] = p47.day,
		["hour"] = p47.hour or 0,
		["min"] = p47.min or 0,
		["sec"] = p47.sec or 0
	})
	local v49 = os.time() - v48
	if v49 < 60 then
		return "Just now"
	end
	if v49 < 3600 then
		local v50 = v49 / 60
		return math.floor(v50) .. " min ago"
	end
	if v49 < 86400 then
		local v51 = v49 / 3600
		return math.floor(v51) .. " hours ago"
	end
	if v49 < 172800 then
		return "Yesterday"
	end
	local v52 = v49 / 86400
	return math.floor(v52) .. " days ago"
end
local function v_u_61(p54) -- name: GetLogTime
	if type(p54) == "string" then
		local v55, v56, v57, v58, v59, v60 = p54:match("(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+):(%d+):(%d+)")
		if not v55 then
			return os.time()
		end
		p54 = {
			["year"] = tonumber(v55),
			["month"] = tonumber(v56),
			["day"] = tonumber(v57),
			["hour"] = tonumber(v58),
			["min"] = tonumber(v59),
			["sec"] = tonumber(v60)
		}
	elseif type(p54) ~= "table" then
		return os.time()
	end
	return os.time({
		["year"] = p54.year,
		["month"] = p54.month,
		["day"] = p54.day,
		["hour"] = p54.hour or 0,
		["min"] = p54.min or 0,
		["sec"] = p54.sec or 0
	})
end

										v_u_5.Notify("ERROR", "The player already owns this gamepass", v_u_6.UI_Error)
									end
								else
									v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, v23)
									return
								end
							else
								v_u_5.Notify("ERROR", "This gamepass cannot be gifted", v_u_6.UI_Error)
								return
							end
						end
					else
						local v25 = v_u_9:FindFirstChild("_" .. v20)
						if v25 and v25.Value == 1 or v_u_2:UserOwnsGamePassAsync(v_u_9.UserId, v20) then
							v_u_5.Notify("ERROR", "You already owns this gamepass", v_u_6.UI_Error)
						else
							v_u_2:PromptGamePassPurchase(v_u_9, v20)
						end
					end
				end
				if v_u_12:GetAttribute("Case") then
					v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, v_u_4.PaidCases[v_u_12:GetAttribute("Case")][v_u_18])
					return
				end
				v_u_2:PromptProductPurchase(v_u_9, v20)
			end
		end)
	end
end

function getRandomRotation(p83, p84) -- name: getRandomRotation
	local v85 = p83 > 0.75 and 0.75 or p83
	local v86 = math.random() * (p84 and v85 and v85 or 1 - v85)
	local v87 = p84 and v86 and v86 or 1 - v86
	local v88 = math.sqrt(v87)
	local v89 = math.asin(v88) * 2
	local v90 = p84 and 3.141592653589793 + v89 or 3.141592653589793 - v89
	local v91 = math.deg(v90)
	if math.random(1, 2) == 1 then
		v91 = 360 - v91
	end
	return v91
end

	local v7 = tostring(p6)
	repeat
		local v8
		v7, v8 = string.gsub(v7, "^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", "%1,%2")

end

		v_u_9.Receiving.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(0.196078, 1, 0.137255)
		v_u_7.Progress.Visible = true
		for v101 = 1, 30 do
			v_u_7.Progress.Txt.Text = (30 - v101) / 10 .. "s"
			task.wait(0.1)
		end
		task.wait(1)
		v_u_7.Progress.Visible = false
		return
	elseif p58 == "ResetConfirm" then
		v_u_35 = false
		v_u_14.Txt.Text = "Confirm"
		v_u_9.Offering.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(0.305882, 0.298039, 0.309804)
		v_u_9.Receiving.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(0.305882, 0.298039, 0.309804)
		print(v_u_9.Offering.UIStroke.Color, v_u_9.Receiving.UIStroke.Color)
		return
	elseif p58 == "Ended" then
		v_u_8.Enabled = false
		for _, v102 in v_u_11.Parent.Currency:GetChildren() do
			if v102:IsA("Frame") then
				v102:Destroy()
			end
		end
		for _, v103 in v_u_10.Parent.Currency:GetChildren() do
			if v103:IsA("Frame") then
				v103:Destroy()
			end
		end
		v_u_5.Notify("TRADE", "The trade was completed successfully", v_u_6.UI_Cash)
		return
	elseif p58 == "Cancel" then
		v_u_8.Enabled = false
		for _, v104 in v_u_11.Parent.Currency:GetChildren() do
			if v104:IsA("Frame") then
				v104:Destroy()
			end
		end
		for _, v105 in v_u_10.Parent.Currency:GetChildren() do
			if v105:IsA("Frame") then
				v105:Destroy()
			end
		end
		v_u_5.Notify("TRADE", "The trade was cancelled", v_u_6.UI_Error2)
	elseif p58 == "Error" then
		v_u_8.Enabled = false
		for _, v106 in v_u_11.Parent.Currency:GetChildren() do
			if v106:IsA("Frame") then
				v106:Destroy()
			end
		end
		for _, v107 in v_u_10.Parent.Currency:GetChildren() do
			if v107:IsA("Frame") then
				v107:Destroy()
			end
		end
		v_u_5.Notify("TRADE", "Something went wrong", v_u_6.UI_BLose)
	end
end)

local function v_u_26(p23, p24) -- name: getRelativeVelocity
	if p23 then
		local v25 = p23.ActiveController and (not (p23.ActiveController:IsA("GroundController") and p23.GroundSensor) and p23.ActiveController:IsA("ClimbController"))
		if v25 then
			v25 = p23.ClimbSensor
		end
		if v25 and v25.SensedPart then
			return p24 - v25.SensedPart:GetVelocityAtPosition(p23.RootPart.Position)
		else
			return p24
		end
	else
		return p24
	end
end

local v_u_104 = {}
local function v_u_106(p105) -- name: characterAdded
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_103
	v_u_103:bindRoot(p105)
end
local function v_u_108(p107) -- name: characterRemoving
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_103
	v_u_103:unbindRoot(p107)
end
local function v115(p109) -- name: playerAdded
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_104, (copy) v_u_103, (copy) v_u_106, (copy) v_u_108
	local v110 = v_u_104[p109]
	if not v110 then
		v110 = {}
		v_u_104[p109] = v110
	end
	if p109.Character then
		v_u_103:bindRoot(p109.Character)
	end
	local v111 = p109.CharacterAdded
	local v112 = v_u_106
	table.insert(v110, v111:Connect(v112))
	local v113 = p109.CharacterRemoving
	local v114 = v_u_108
	table.insert(v110, v113:Connect(v114))
end
local function v119(p116) -- name: playerRemoving
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_104, (copy) v_u_103
	local v117 = v_u_104[p116]
	if v117 then
		for _, v118 in ipairs(v117) do
			v118:Disconnect()
		end
		v_u_104[p116] = nil
	end
	if p116.Character then
		v_u_103:unbindRoot(p116.Character)
	end
end
for _, v120 in ipairs(v_u_1:GetPlayers()) do
	task.spawn(v115, v120)
end
v_u_1.PlayerAdded:Connect(v115)
v_u_1.PlayerRemoving:Connect(v119)
local v_u_1 = {}
v_u_1.__index = v_u_1
function v_u_1.new() -- name: new
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	local v2 = v_u_1
	local v3 = setmetatable({}, v2)
	v3.cameras = require(script:WaitForChild("CameraModule"))
	v3.controls = require(script:WaitForChild("ControlModule"))
	return v3
end
function v_u_1.GetCameras(p4) -- name: GetCameras
	return p4.cameras
end
function v_u_1.GetControls(p5) -- name: GetControls
	return p5.controls
end
function v_u_1.GetClickToMoveController(p6) -- name: GetClickToMoveController
	return p6.controls:GetClickToMoveController()
end
return v_u_1.new()
